EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_SPELLSIZE=- Report current memory usage of the spell checker
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_DICE=(count = 1) (sides = 6) - Return a random value equivalent to rolling the given number of dice with the given number of sides
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_BROWSE=- Open the archive browser for viewing files in the game data archives
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_FILECOUNT=(directory) - Count the total number of files contained within given directory on disk (recursive)
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_ELIZA=- Chat with Eliza. Enter 'stop' or 'exit' when done.
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_VARGET=(variable) - Display the current variable value

EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_VARLIST=- List all variables and their values
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_REGLIST=- List all existing editor registry groups
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_REGCOPY=(src) (dst) - Copy an editor registry group
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_REGMOVE=(src) (dst) - Move an editor registry group
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_REGDELETE=(group) - Delete an editor registry group
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_VIDMEM=- Display video memory usage statistics
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_SYSMEM=- Display system memory usage statistics
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_MEMWINDOW=- Toggle display of the memory usage statistics window
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_CAMERASHAKE=(amplitude) (frequency) (random factor) (duration) (direction = <x><y><z>) (position = <eye><target><both>) - Shake the Terrain Editor camera
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_CAMERAMULTIPLY=(field) (factor) - Multiply the camera field value by a factor for all selected cameras in the current map (use with no arguments for a list of field codes)
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_CLIFFINFO=- Toggle display of cliff information in the Terrain Editor status bar
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_BNETLOGIN=- - Log in to Blizzard (using settings from preferences)
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_BNETLOGOUT=- - Log out of Blizzard
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_BNETSTATUS=- - Report current Blizzard connection status
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_LOCALE=(locale code) - Change the editor locale
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_GAME=- Invoke a game cheat command
EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_TEXUVGET=- Display the texture uv tiling values for the current terrain

EDSTR_CONSOLEHELP_DIFF=(file 1) (file 2) - Display differences between two files

// Hints
EDSTR_HINT_TITLE=Hint
EDSTR_HINT_DONTSHOW=Do not show this hint again
EDSTR_HINT_ACTORPASTE=You are about to create a copy of an object referenced in Actor data.<N/><N/>This object will not appear in game, nor will it trigger audio or visual effects in game unless you modify Actor data.<N/><N/>Refer to the editor documentation for a more detailed explanation of why this is necessary.

// Tips
EDSTR_TIP_TITLE=Editor Tips
EDSTR_TIP_SHOWONSTARTUP=Show Tips When Starting Up
EDSTR_TIP_NEXT=Next Tip
EDSTR_TIP_PREV=Previous Tip

EDSTR_TIP_001=To use units from the single player campaign, add the 'Liberty (Campaign)' dependency to your document using the 'Add Standard' button in the Dependencies dialog.<N/><N/>(File > Dependencies...)
EDSTR_TIP_002=If the Terrain module seems sluggish, try reducing the video settings in the editor preferences.<N/><N/>(File > Preferences... > Video)
EDSTR_TIP_003=Trigger libraries defined in Mod files can be automatically loaded by adding the library id to the 'Trigger Libraries - Identifier' field within the 'Default SC2 Gameplay Settings' in the Data module (under the Gameplay Data type).
EDSTR_TIP_004=To run your map in the game, you can either use the Test Document command, or publish the map to Blizzard services.<N/><N/>(File > Test Document)<N/>(File > Publish...)
EDSTR_TIP_005=You can import your own images or sounds with the Import module, and then use those within the Data and Trigger modules.
EDSTR_TIP_006=The trigger function 'Players On Team' returns players associated with teams set up in the Blizzard game lobby.
EDSTR_TIP_007=Take a break from making maps and chat with Eliza.<N/><N/>(Window > Console)
EDSTR_TIP_008=You can pre-define unit groups for use in Triggers using the Object Groups dialog.<N/><N/>(Map > Object Groups...)
EDSTR_TIP_009=The game categories listed for your map on Blizzard services, such as Melee or Custom, come from the Game Variants defined in the map.<N/><N/>(Map > Game Variants...)
EDSTR_TIP_010=The in-game Trigger Debugging Window can be very useful for tracking down problems with your triggers.<N/><N/>(File > Preferences... > Test Document)
EDSTR_TIP_011=When painting textures along cliff edges, the 'Same Cliff Level Only' option will prevent the texture from also being applied to the other side of the cliff.<N/><N/>(Tools > Brush > Same Cliff Level Only)
EDSTR_TIP_012=The 'Export Map Image' command in the Terrain module can be used to save out high quality screenshots of your entire map.<N/><N/>(Data > Export Map Image...)
EDSTR_TIP_013=Custom Script elements can be used in the Trigger module to enter any script code you want, and you can even use them to 'include' additional script files imported using the Import module.<N/><N/>(Data > New > New Custom Script)
EDSTR_TIP_014=The Overview Manager can be useful for finding out where individual objects or trigger elements are being used in the document.
EDSTR_TIP_015=The trigger function 'Player Score Value' can be used to access all of the score values tracked automatically by the game, including things like 'Enemy Units Killed' and 'Minerals Gathered'.
EDSTR_TIP_016=The smallest time interval that a trigger can wait is 1/16 of a second (0.0625 seconds), which is equivalent to one game loop.
EDSTR_TIP_017=Type 'help' at the editor console to see a list of commands that can be used there.<N/><N/>(Window > Console)
EDSTR_TIP_018=Use the 'Manage Published' window to view or remove maps and mods you have previously published to Blizzard services.<N/><N/>(File > Manage Published...)
EDSTR_TIP_019=You can configure the editor to automatically save and backup your documents.<N/><N/>(File > Preferences... > Documents)
EDSTR_TIP_020=Use adjust commands in the Terrain module to tweak object placement in small, precise increments.<N/><N/>(Edit > Adjust)
EDSTR_TIP_021=Multiple regions can be merged together and treated as a single region.<N/><N/>(Edit > Merge Selection)
EDSTR_TIP_022=To allow different cliff types to be placed on top of each other or connected together, enable the 'Allow Cliff Merging' option.<N/><N/>(Tools > Brush > Allow Cliff Merging)
EDSTR_TIP_023=Hotkeys for all commands in the editor can be customized, including adding hotkeys to commands that don't have one by default.<N/><N/>(File > Configure Controls...)
EDSTR_TIP_024=The Text module can perform basic spell checking on all text used in your map or mod.<N/><N/>(Data > Spell Check...)
EDSTR_TIP_025=The Duplicate command in the Data module allows you to selectively duplicate or share any linked objects.<N/><N/>(Data > Duplicate...)
EDSTR_TIP_026=The Object Explorer display in the Data module provides access to all objects linked to by the current object.<N/><N/>(View > Show Object Explorer)
EDSTR_TIP_027=Use the Explain Link command with the Object Explorer display in the Data module to see exactly which fields are linking to the object.<N/><N/>(Data > Explain Link)
EDSTR_TIP_028=Advanced fields are optional in the Data module. Hide them to keep things simple, or show them to see every possible field.<N/><N/>(View > Show Advanced Values)
EDSTR_TIP_029=In the Data module, lists corresponding to sub-fields within the same structure can be displayed together in a single list.<N/><N/>(View > Combine Structure Values)
EDSTR_TIP_030=To view objects, fields, and values in the Data module using their internal data instead of more descriptive text, enable Raw Data display.<N/><N/>(View > View Raw Data)
EDSTR_TIP_031=In the Data module, the object list can be displayed as either a sortable list view, or a tree view grouped by categories.<N/><N/>(View > Display Object List As Tree)
EDSTR_TIP_032=The Unit data type represents any object in the game world which can affect gameplay, including mobile units, buildings, missiles, destructible objects, and pathing blockers.
EDSTR_TIP_033=The Actor data type represents any visual object or effect in the game world, and are generally associated with Units or Effects.
EDSTR_TIP_034=The Ability data type represents actions which can be performed by Units, usually through buttons on the command card.
EDSTR_TIP_035=The Weapon data type represents types of attacks performed by Units.
EDSTR_TIP_036=The Behavior data type represents passive effects or states that may be applied to Units.
EDSTR_TIP_037=The Effect data type represents individual visual or gameplay effects which are used to define Abilities and Behaviors.

// Cheats
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Ally=Changes all alliance states between the selected players. By default, if you just type Ally, then all players share all alliance states with you.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceDefeat=Changes the Defeat alliance state between the selected players. By default, if you just type AllianceDefeat, all players will share defeat with you.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceControl=Changes the Control alliance state between the selected players. By default, if you just type AllianceControl, then all players share control with you.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceGiveHelp=Changes the GiveHelp alliance state between the selected players. By default, if you just type AllianceGiveHelp, all players will respond to calls for help from your units.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AlliancePassive=Changes the Passive alliance state between the selected players. Players that you are not passive with will be considered hostile for attacking purposes.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AlliancePushable=Changes the Pushable alliance state between the selected players. This controls whether a player’s units will move through another player’s units, pushing them out of the way.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceSeekHelp=Changes the SeekHelp alliance state between the selected players. Controls whether a player’s units call for help to the specified target player. The target player can choose to respond or not, depending on its GiveHelp alliance setting.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceSpend=Changes the Spend alliance state between the selected players. Players that you are sharing resources with are allowed to spend your money to purchase things.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceTrade=Changes the Trade alliance state between the selected players. Players that you are trading with can be sent resources.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceVision=Changes the Vision alliance state between the selected players.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_BehaviorAdd=Adds the requested behavior to the selected units.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_BehaviorDuration=Sets the duration of the requested behavior.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_BehaviorRemove=Removes the requested behavior from the selected units.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Charges=Toggles spell charge validation.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Cooldown=Toggles spell cooldown validation.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Creep=Adds creep at the cursor position given the requested radius.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_DamageDealt=Multiplies the amount of damage dealt by a player’s units by the specified value.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_DamageTaken=Multiplies the amount of damage taken by a player’s units by the specified value.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_DeathAll=Kills all units on the map. Units will perform their normal death activities, which could result in units being spawned in response to their parent’s death.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_DeathExcept=Kills all units on the map except the selected units. Units will perform their normal death activities, which could result in units being spawned in response to their parent’s death.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_DeathSide=Kills all the units owned by the selected player. Units will perform their normal death activities, which could result in units being spawned in response to their parent’s death.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_DeathUnit=Kills the selected units. Units will perform their normal death activities, which could result in units being spawned in response to their parent’s death.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Defeat=Ends the game in defeat for the selected player.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_DestroyPersistent=Destroys all persistent effects within the specified radius of the cursor.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Effect=Executes the requested effect from the selected units.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_FastBuild=Toggles fast building, research, and training times.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_FastHeal=Toggles fast healing times.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Fidget=Forces selected units to perform the specified fidget type.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Food=Toggles food usage validation.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Free=Toggles cost validation and expenditure.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_God=Turns on god mode for the selected player. Units owned by players that are in god mode will deal amplified damage, and take no damage.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Loot=Drops a type of loot for the specified player.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_MakeUnit=Creates N units for the specified player. Units will be created around the cursor position, or in the center of the map if the cursor position is invalid.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Minerals=Adds the specified amount of minerals to the selected player.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Move=Moves the selected units to the cursor position.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_NoDefeat=Disables defeat conditions.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_NoVictory=Disables victory conditions.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Order=Orders the selected units to use an ability.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Owner=Changes ownership for the selected units to the selected player.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_ResourceCustom=Adds the specified amount of a custom resource to the specified player
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_SetAll=Sets the life, shields, mana, and scrap of the selected units to the specified value.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_SetEnergy=Sets the energy of the selected units to the specified value.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_SetLife=Sets the hitpoints of the selected units to the specified value.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_SetShields=Sets the shields of the selected units to the specified value.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_SetResource=Sets the resources of the selected units to the specified value.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Showmap=Toggles fog of war display and validation.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Techtree=Toggles tech tree dependency validation.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Terrazine=Adds the specified amount of Terrazine to the specified player
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Tie=Marks all undecided players with the tie result.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_TimeOfDay=Sets the time of day to the specified time.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_TimeOfDayRate=Sets the rate that the time of day changes to the specified value.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_TrigDebug=Opens the trigger debug window
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_TrigRun=Runs the specified trigger
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Uncreep=Removes creep at the cursor position given the requested radius.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Undecided=Marks the selected player's result as undecided.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Upgrade=Applies the selected upgrade to the selected player.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Vespene=Adds the specified amount of vespene gas to the specified player
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_Victory=Ends the game in defeat for all players that don't share the defeat alliance state with the selected player.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_XP=Adds a relative amount of XP to the selected units. This can be used to change veterancy levels.
